reset
set term svg enhanced background rgb 'white'
set datafile separator ','
set title '2021-01-01'
set output 'graph/2021-01-01.svg'
set xtics format '%H:%M'
set ytics ('0   0'0,'10  20'20,'20  40'40,'30  60'60,'40  80'80,'50 100'100)
set y2tics (0,200,400,600,800,1000)
set yrange [0:100]
set y2range [0:1000]
set xlabel 'time(Hour)'
set ylabel 'Temperature (°C) / Humidity (%)'
set y2label 'CO2 (ppm)'
set size ratio 0.5625
set xdata time
set timefmt '%H:%M:%S'
set grid
